            endpoint = {"commandMetadata":{"webCommandMetadata":{"url":"/channel/UCOmHUn--16B90oW2L6FRR3A","webPageType":"WEB_PAGE_TYPE_BROWSE","rootVe":3611}},"urlEndpoint":{"url":"/channel/UCOmHUn--16B90oW2L6FRR3A"}};

              page: "browse",
